We take on big problems to help drivers, riders, delivery partners, and eaters get moving in more than 600 cities around the world.   "text_content": "Staff Scientist, Tech - Bangalore, India | Uber Careers Please enable Javascript Please enable Javascript Skip to main content Staff Scientist, Tech Data Scientist, Data Science in Bangalore, India Apply Now About the team The Core Analytics & Science Team (CAS) is Uber's primary science organisation, covering both our main lines of business as well as the underlying platform technologies on which those businesses are built. We are a key part of Uber's cross-functional product development teams, helping to drive every stage of product development through data analytic, statistical, and algorithmic expertise. CAS owns the experience and algorithms powering Uber's global Mobility and Delivery products. We optimise and personalise the rider and driver experience, target incentives and introduce customizations for routing and matching for products and use cases that go beyond the core Uber capabilities. About the Role You'll be the Science Tech Lead (Individual Contributor) for a team of 5-7 members based in India, working closely with Engineering and Product leads to create and execute the direction of the product development. This includes crafting machine learning, statistics, or analytical solutions to achieve business goals, guiding the team's direction through data-driven insights and algorithmic thinking, mentoring scientists and establishing cross functional relationships with partner teams at different locations. Basic Qualifications Undergraduate and/or graduate degree in Statistics, Machine Learning, Operations Research, or other quantitative fields. 9+ years of industry experience as an (Applied / Data) Scientist or equivalent. Experience with exploratory data analysis, statistical analysis and testing, causal analysis and ML model development. Experience in experimental design and analysis. Proficiency using Python, Spark at scale with large data sets. Experience with tools like SQL, R in a production environment. Preferred Qualifications Master’s/Ph.D. Degree in Statistics, Machine Learning, Operations Research, or other quantitative fields. Experience in tech or marketplace industries. Experienced in partnering with cross-functional stakeholders to execute decisions. Ability to mentor, coach and develop junior team members. Superb communication and organisation skills. What the candidate will do Collaborate with Engineering and Product leadership to define the technical vision and guide team direction by identifying opportunities and creating data-driven solutions. Design innovative solutions and develop prototypes for business challenges using machine learning and statistical algorithms. Establish and guide data analysis and experimentation frameworks to generate business insights and support decision-making. Work closely with Engineering and Product teams to deploy models, improve data observability and metrics, and execute experiments and detailed analyses. Design and evaluate A/B tests, switchback experiments and quasi-experiments, applying best practices in experimental methodology to ensure high-quality, unbiased insights. Partner with Scientists and Engineers to build and enhance the availability, integrity, accuracy, and reliability of data logging and data pipelines. Provide mentorship and technical leadership to other Scientists, promoting a culture of statistical excellence and continuous learning. Communicate effectively with leadership and cross-functional teams, presenting the Science team's work on models, solutions, and data analytics outcomes. You will be enabling greater coordination, efficiency, and velocity across the org and act as a change agent to help the organization shift from being an internal-only focused team to a business line. The ideal candidate for this role has strong analytical skills, excellent time-management and organizational habits, experience navigating and influencing a cross-functional, matrix organization, and the ability to clearly communicate and present information to senior stakeholders. We're looking for someone who can zoom out to set a vision and solve problems from 30,000 feet, as well as zoom in to dive deep into the details! This role reports to the Head of GSS. What You Will Do: Top-down strategy refresh: Co-create and maintain GSS top-down strategy document along with GSS steering committee (leadership team) Governance and rhythm of operations: Set governance processes, manage rhythm and cadence of operations for the entire business. MBA or degree in business/analytics/economics Strong project management and governance expertise Strong analytical and quantitative skills, proficient with Excel, Google Sheets, Dashboards, presentations etc Self-starter - the ability to self-serve, investigate and get the data we require will make you much more effective in this role You never hesitate to roll up your sleeves and address something hands-on, you persevere and remain resilient. Comfortable with ambiguity; the ability to structure ideas into actionable plans Experience in a high-growth environment Strong stakeholder management and interpersonal skills with exposure to senior leadership, cross-functional teams and global teams Preferred Qualifications: Excellent written (decks, papers) and verbal communication skills with exceptional emotional intelligence. Superior organizational skills with the ability to juggle many tasks without losing sight of the highest priority items. Strong bias towards action. You drive end-to-end results and are always thinking ahead. Attention to detail and you are constantly looking for ways to tweak and optimize for better results.
